description</div></div><div class="YgLbBe"><div jscontroller="GCSbhd" jsaction="rcuQ6b:npT2md"><style>.WbZuDe{display:none}.config-text-expandable .WbZuDe{display:inline}.UiMktc{display:inline}.config-text-expandable .UiMktc{display:none}.CdXzFe{cursor:pointer}.j4kHIf{color:#2111da;font-size:14px;margin-top:18px}.config-text-expandable .CdXzFe{display:none}.cVLgvc{vertical-align:middle}.tbKN6d{vertical-align:middle}.Wc7XP{margin-left:8px}</style><span class="HBvzbc" style="line-height:1.5em">Company / Location Information

Water technology is one of the fastest-growing industries in the world. As a leading global water technology company, A. O. Smith Corporation (NYSE: AOS) is at the center of the trend. We are a $4 billion company with over 140 years of history and 12,000+ employees. Our emphasis is on hot water and clean water; we are one of the world's largest manufacturers of<span class="UiMktc">...</span><span class="WbZuDe"> residential and commercial water heating equipment as well as a supplier of water purification products in a number of emerging countries.

With manufacturing operations in the United States, Canada, Mexico, China, India, and Europe, we have the reach to serve customers worldwide.

A.O. Smith is committed to continuous improvement and maintaining a culture that values and respects our employees. Recognized by The Tennessean as one of the top Nashville area Workplaces, we have programs in place to help our team members achieve their potential. When you join our team, you will receive rewards and recognition for your contributions, training and professional development opportunities, as well as a variety of benefits to support you and your family's health, well-being, and financial future. If you are inspired to learn, take risks, and succeed as a team, you can build an amazing career at A. O. Smith

This role is located in our modern Nashville Metro Center office, located just minutes from downtown with easy interstate access and free parking.

This role is eligible for a remote work schedule of up to two days remote work per week. New employees are eligible to apply after successfully completing their initial 90 days of employment and training.

Primary Function

Design, develop, document, test, and debug new and existing software systems and/or applications (cloud and/or in-house). Serve as technical expert on development projects. Participate in full development life cycle including requirements analysis and design. Write technical specifications based on conceptual design and stated business requirements. Entry level position within field. Conducts routine tasks as directed.

Responsibilities
• Support, maintain, and document software functionality.
• Identify and evaluate new technologies for implementation.
• Analyze code to find causes of errors and revise programs as needed.
• Participate in software design meetings and analyze user needs to determine technical requirements.
• Consult with end user to prototype, refine, test, and debug programs to meet needs.
• Provides application software development services or technical support typically in a defined project.
• Develops program logic for new applications or analyzes and modifies logic in existing applications.
• Codes, tests, debugs, documents, implements and maintains software applications.
• Analyzes requirements, and maintains, tests and integrates application components.
• Ensures that system improvements are successfully implemented.
• Develops competence by performing structured work assignments.
• Uses existing procedures to solve routine or standard problems.
• Receives instruction, guidance and direction from others
• May be involved in website planning and deployment.
• Writes technical documentation regarding the website's or other technical requirements.
• Provides application software development services or technical support typically in a defined project.
• Develops program logic for new applications or analyzes and modifies logic in existing applications.
• Perform other duties as assigned.

Qualifications
• Recent graduate with Bachelor's Degree in Computer Science MIS (or related field) or Software Development School graduate; candidates with equivalent years of related IT experience, certifications, and education also considered
• 1+ year related work experience
• Advanced computer skills including programming experience
• Demonstrated exceptional written and oral communication skills
• Excellent communication skills via written and oral.
• Proficiency in Microsoft Office Suite; Word, Excel, Access, Outlook, etc.

We Offer

Competitive compensation package and comprehensive benefits plans which include medical and dental insurance, company-sponsored life insurance, retirement security savings plan, short- and long-term • Performs code reviews.
• Performs system maintenance and enhancements.

• 8+ years’ .Net experience
• 8+ years’ C# experience
• SQL DB
• JIRA Experience

• X.12 medical claims (837, 834, 277, etc)

Experience with T-SQL

Citizenship Requirement

Security Clearance Requirements

U.S. Citizenship required for this specific opportunity

Must possess or qualify for a Public Trust (MBI)

CRITICAL NOTES:
• SSG will not make assumptions regarding your qualifications. Your answers to the mandatory screening questions must be supported by the information on your resume. Applications with inconsistencies will not be considered.
• Recruiters or Third parties will not be considered.
• This is a 100% U.S. based remote position. However, candidates from CA, CO, NJ or NY will not be considered.
• This is a 1099 position

U.S Citizenship is required for this specific opportunity. Applicants selected will be subject to a government security investigation and must meet eligibility requirements for access to classified information and be able to obtain a government-granted security clearance. Individuals may also be subject to a background investigation including, but not limited to criminal history, employment and education verification, drug testing, and creditworthiness.

Syms Strategic Group, LLC is an Equal Opportunity Employer. Qualified applicants will receive consideration for employment without regard to race, color, religion, sex, age, national origin, marital status, disability, veteran status, sexual orientation, or genetic information.

description</div></div><div class="YgLbBe"><div jscontroller="GCSbhd" jsaction="rcuQ6b:npT2md"><span class="HBvzbc" style="line-height:1.5em">Lead Application Developer

Required Location: Tampa, FL or Nashville/Hermitage, TN<span class="UiMktc">...</span><span class="WbZuDe">

Are you passionate about technology and interested in joining a community of collaborative colleagues who respectfully and courageously seek to challenge the status quo? If so, read on to learn more about an exciting opportunity with Deloitte's Information Technology Services (ITS). We are insatiably curious and life-long learners focused on technology and innovation.

Work you'll do

A unique opportunity to be a part of growing DAS team that drives consistency, quality, and efficiency of the services delivered to various internal and external clients. You will be responsible for delivering Web Application solutions to support Deloitte Member Firm. Additional responsibilities include designing, deploying and supporting custom products and complex workflows.

Technical Skills:

• Good analytical skills to understand the requirements and lead the team for removing technical roadblocks and also perform hands on coding

• Soft skills needed: Self-starter, proactive, approachable, solution oriented, team player

• Good knowledge or working experience in Agile and/or SAFe projects

• Work experience in designing modules, estimation, task management for self and team

• Strong trouble-shooting skills to resolve technical issues

• Very strong in web development which includes .NET Platform(4.8), .Net Core, ASP.NET MVC (4.0 / 5.0), Angular, HTML, HTML 5, CSS.

• Very strong in C# as development language, .NET framework concepts and implementation and OOPs concepts

• Very Strong SQL Server (includes working with DML, DDL, Stored procedures,)

• Strong in services development and hosting for WCF, ASP.NET Web API

• Strong in writing automated unit testing code

• Strong in SSIS, SSRS.

• Experience with core AWS services such as:

o Step functions

o serverless approach: AWS Lambda services

o Storage services: Amazon S3

o Security: AWS Key Management service, AWS IAM

Monitoring &amp; Management: AWS CloudWatch

• Working experience on Performance Tuning of an application using C# and SQL

• Used Application Blocks like logging, exception handling, etc.

• Have worked with 3rd-party web controls

• Demonstrate ability to apply Microsoft Practices and Patterns

• Ability to provide debugging and troubleshooting help

Support:

• Provide consultative support in designing web applications solutions

• Support QA team with clarifications/ doubts

• Delivery and deployment of the projects to different environments

• Liaise with a learning group to provide input into training materials

• Provide input to standards and guidelines and implement best practices to enable consistency across all projects

• Participate in the continuous improvement processes, as assigned

The Team

Information Technology Services (ITS) helps power Deloitte's success. ITS is the engine that drives Deloitte, which serves many of the world's largest, most respected organizations. We develop and deploy cutting-edge internal and go-to-market solutions that help Deloitte operate effectively and lead in the market. Our reputation is built on a tradition of delivering with excellence.

The 2,200 professionals in ITS deliver services including:

• Security, risk &amp; compliance

• Technology support

• Infrastructure

• Applications

• Relationship management

• Strategy

• Deployment

• PMO

• Financials

• Communications

Deloitte Application Studios (DAS)

Deloitte Application Studios (DAS) is the internal software and applications development team responsible for delivering leading-edge technologies to Deloitte professionals. Their broad portfolio includes web and mobile productivity tools which empower our people to log expenses, enter timesheets, book travel and more, anywhere, anytime. DAS enables our client service professionals through a comprehensive suite of applications across the business lines. In addition to application delivery, DAS offers full-scale design services, a robust mobile portfolio, cutting-edge analytics, and innovative custom development.

Qualifications

Required Qualifications:

• Minimum of 8+ years of related experience as a full stack developer with a Bachelor Degree in Computer Science or related field or 5 years of related experience with an advanced degree

• Technical experience and expertise in the following:

o React with Redux, Typescript, Node JS, Socket IO

o .NET Framework &amp; .NET Core

o Azure PaaS services - app services, APIM, Redis, App Insights, etc.

o Azure SQL and Cosmos

o AWS

o C#

o DDD with Event based distributed architecture

• Ability to travel 20%, monthly travel of 3-4 days to Tampa/Hermitage

• Limited immigration sponsorship may be available

Preferred Qualifications:

• Experience with leading a scrum team

• Excellent written and verbal communication skills with strong attention to detail

• Strong problem-solving skills

• Ability to communicate to business leaders

Job Title: C#.NET Software Engineer
Pay Rate: $35 to 37/Hr
Duration: 12 Months
Location: Johnson City, TN (On-Site)

This position is for the Factory Automation division.

C#.NET Software Engineer's primary responsibility will be to develop and test Software solutions on a Windows-based C# desktop application.

The job will be 5 days a week (40 hours) in the office, in Johnson City, TN for the first several months. After that, there can be a negotiation about splitting time (say 3 days a week in the office). But fully remote work, from day 1, is not an option.
• Develops software.
• Reviews relevant requirements, standards, and other documentation to clarify and understand software engineering requirements.
• Provides estimates for modules under development, and estimates own work.
• Completes the development of software test requirements for modules under development.
• Executes software (unit and integration) tests.
• Presents technical findings and developments.
• Adheres to the software quality process through the execution of module, subsystem, and system test procedures.
• Analyzes localization requirements and designs/adapts products and solutions accordingly.
• Agile/Lean software development process.

Requirements:
• BS Computer Science or Computer Engineering
• Demonstrate good interpersonal, communication, and teamwork skills
• Proficient in C# programming language and object-oriented design methodology (NOT SELF-TAUGHT)
• Self-motivated and results-oriented

Job Types: Full-time, Contract

Salary: $35.00 - $37.00 per hour

Experience level:
• 2 years

Schedule:
• 8 hour shift

Ability to commute/relocate:
• Johnson City, TN 37604: Reliably commute or planning to relocate before starting work (Required)

Application Question(s):
• This is a W2 position
• please provide your email address

Education:
• Bachelor's (Required)

Experience:
• C#.Net: 2 years (Required)
• OOP: 2 years (Required)

description</div></div><div class="YgLbBe"><div jscontroller="GCSbhd" jsaction="rcuQ6b:npT2md"><span class="HBvzbc" style="line-height:1.5em">Live IT Up at Ciber Global
At Ciber Global, we believe the most inspired, innovative and industrious companies should win, regardless of size or legacy. We're the small company that cares and the big company that can. We deliver breakthrough performances and powerful solutions that are anything but cookie cutter in order to give our clients the competitive advantage they deserve.
Work<span class="UiMktc">...</span><span class="WbZuDe">
Role Description:
Ciber Global is seeking a .Net developer that will be responsible for providing software development and maintenance of applications for corporate initiatives in Nashville, TN.
Responsibilities:
Development responsibilities will include providing solutions that follow development standards, integrate with other systems and that fulfill business requirements.
Responsibilities will include system enhancements, new system code development, web-based and windows-based application development, systems conversions, reporting services and other technical efforts requiring software development.
Provide production support of business applications, which includes resolving issues and removing defects by priority and severity.
Develop software solutions following established development standards.
Develop software that integrates with other systems.
Participate in planning and prioritization sessions and provide estimates.
Unit test each software component to ensure business requirements are fulfilled.
Ensure that all application artifacts are archived in a code repository.
Complete assignments in a timely and accurate manner and proactively escalate any risks to management.
Provide consistent and concise status reports as requested by management.
Perform other duties and job functions as requested by management.
Skills/
Experience:
5 years of experience in software development for business systems
Bachelor's degree or equivalent experience
Must have experience in ASP.NET, C#, JavaScript, jQuery, Visual Studio, Ajax, SSRS, SQL Server, Responsive Web Design and TFS Working knowledge of agile methodologies and software development lifecycles
Must have strong written communication, analytical, and interpersonal skills
This position requires the successful completion of a background investigation and/or drug screen.
Ciber Global is an Equal Opportunity Employer Minorities/Females/Gender Identity/Sexual Orientation/Protected Veterans/Individuals with Disabilities.
Learn.
Talent Services bring clients a range of staffing solutions, from a single contractor to a team of experts to help achieve their key business goals on target and within budget. Our talent sourcing model uncovers the right IT talent and aligns critical skills with client technology, culture, and expectations.
Grow.
Ciber Global is an IT consulting company who partners with organizations to develop technology strategies and solutions that deliver tangible business value. Founded in 1974, Ciber is an HTC Global Services company. For more information, visit www.Ciber.com.

Data SQL .net Product - Onsite Posted on Dec 22, 2021 Apply for this job your email: upload resume:
Profile

Title:

VP of Technology - Hands-on Leader:
Data, SQL, .net, Product

Location:

Nashville, TNSalary: $120,,000 Bonus Leads and directs the Technical Delivery department to ensure strategic and effective use of technology in support of operations and delivery of products and services. Ensures maximum system availability, data integrity and data security. Researches, recommends, and directs the implementation of new/improved technology to further the competitive position.

ESSENTIAL DUTIES AND

RESPONSIBILITIES Directs and manages the technology functions to ensure that systems, networks, hardware and telecommunications operate effectively.

Participates in IT project priority process and offers recommendations on scope and difficulty of proposed projects. Oversees the management of approved IT projects to ensure timely completion, effective testing, coordinated delivery and on-going communication with all stakeholders regarding project status and issues.

Ensures development of processing and backup procedures to safeguard system integrity and facilitate systems recovery. Ensures thorough and regular testing of backup processes. Directs the timely and accurate update of systems documentation and operations manuals.

Develops, updates, and ensures compliance with disaster recovery plans and systems security/loss prevention plans including maintaining active and robust antivirus and firewall protections.

Works with all our technology partners and the internal technology team to develop operational standards for IT functions and processes.

Directs development team in measuring and improving the productivity and efficiency of IT resources against standards. Encourages and implements continuing efficiencies in operational processes and functions.

Ensures timely and accurate diagnosis and resolution of network and system-related issues throughout the technology infrastructure to ensure maximum systems availability. Effectively communicates status of key issues and resolution efforts to Executive Management Team.

Consults with peer executives regarding opportunities to enhance operational efficiency or product delivery. Researches and recommends technology solutions in support of business plans and strategic goals.

Assesses the effectiveness of existing networks and telecommunication systems and recommends updates and changes to maximize efficiency and support future growth or changes within the abreast of changing trends in technology to include hardware, networks and network tools, software, IT security and systems. Uses broad knowledge and perspective to create competitive and breakthrough strategies and plans.

Negotiates cost effective contracts for systems, hardware, software, or peripherals including service warranties, maintenance programs or consultants. Develops effective partnerships with outsourced systems vendors and manages vendor performance against contracts.

Serves as central contact for both internal and external audit of critical systems and coordinates appropriate response to audit concerns. Ensures accurate and complete records of critical systems and systems that the department complies with all applicable federal, state, and local laws and regulations. Develops and revises procedures to assure adherence to established compliance policies

Ensures effective cascading communications throughout the IT department so that critical information, policies, procedures, and announcements are effectively and consistently shared.

Ensures effective collaborative communications between IT department and other divisions/departments so that issues can be resolved quickly and efficiently.

Directs the strategic development and management of the IT department in support

Prepares annual budget for the department and ensures that it operates within budget guidelines and monitors business unit’s performance to operate within DNI financial objectives.

Assists in the creation of technology project budgets for other business lines as needed.

Qualifications
10 to 15 years prior experience as an Information Systems Manager with full scope of responsibility including hardware, software development life cycle, networks, and Product API's2 years’ experience in a medium to large-sized IT department, and has a good knowledge of IT functions, systems, applications, and…</span></span><div class="CdXzFe j4kHIf" data-li="" data-t="config-text-expandable" class="mxts1">Job description</div></div><div class="YgLbBe"><div jscontroller="GCSbhd" jsaction="rcuQ6b:npT2md"><span class="HBvzbc" style="line-height:1.5em">You Matter

• Make a difference every day in the lives of the underserved• Join a mission driven organization with a people first culture• Excellent career growth opportunities<span class="UiMktc">...</span><span class="WbZuDe">

Join us and find a career that supports:• Caring for overlooked, underserved, and vulnerable patients• Diversity, equity, inclusion, and belonging• Autonomy in a warm team environment• Growth and training

Perks and Benefits In addition to comprehensive benefits including medical, dental, vision, paid time off, and 401k, we foster a work, life balance for team members and their family to support physical, mental, and financial wellbeing including: • DailyPay, receive your money as you earn it! • Tuition Assistance and dependent Scholarships• Employee Assistance Program (EAP) including free counseling and health coaching• Company paid life insurance• Tax free Health Spending Accounts (HSA)• Wellness program featuring fitness memberships and product discounts• Preferred banking partnership and discounted rates for home and auto loans

Why Us

Now is your moment to make a difference in the lives of the underserved. If there is one unifying characteristic of everyone on our team, it is the deep desire to make a difference by helping society's most vulnerable and often overlooked individuals. Every day we have the distinct honor and responsibility to show up with non-judgmental compassion to provide hope and healing to those who need it most. For those whose calling it is to serve others, now is your moment to join our mission to provide quality care to every patient with compassion, collaboration, and innovation, to live our mantra to “Always Do The Right Thing!”, and to collectively do our part to heal the world, one patient at a time.

How you make a difference

The role of a Senior AWS Software Engineer involves the implementation, upkeep, and assistance of enterprise-level software applications and databases. Additionally, they oversee both software development projects and the allocation of resources for these endeavors.

Key Responsibilities
• Analyze, define, and document system requirements for data, workflows, logical processes, interfaces, and controls.
• Manage daily operations for multiple projects, consulting with clients, and obtaining approvals.
• Write comprehensive program documentation, including logic, coding, testing, changes, and corrections.
• Provide training, coaching, and maintain professional relationships while promoting teamwork.
• Apply critical thinking, adaptability, and accountability, even under stress, in line with standardized procedures.

Qualifications &amp; Requirements

Education
• Relevant Bachelor’s degree from an accredited college or university. Equivalent experience may be substituted for formal education.

Experience
• 7+ years of professional programming experience.
• Expertise in AWS tools such as Lambda, Step Functions, SQS, Aurora, DynamoDB, API Gateway, and S3.
• Expertise in C#, .Net Core, JavaScript, Angular JS, and SQL.
• Expertise in ASP.NET, WCF, WebAPI, MSMQ, and Nuget is a plus.
• Proven experience creating, executing and completing technical initiatives.
• Advance knowledge in cloud-based design patterns such as microservices, highly scalable frameworks, and strangle the monolith.
• Ability to effectively communicate advanced technical concepts to less experienced members of the development team.
• In-depth understanding of the current Microsoft development suite or similar tools.
• Experience developing browser-based software solutions.

Licenses/Certifications
• None

We are an Equal Employment Opportunity / Affirmative Action Employer

We celebrate diversity and are committed to creating an inclusive environment for all employees.

We encourage you to apply! If you are excited about a role but your experience doesn’t seem to align perfectly with every element of the job description, we encourage you to apply.
